100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那辆大红色铃木125摩托车，凭空消失了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟找遍了本地的二手车贩，这些人不少都是兼职警方特情，没人见过这辆摩托车。这车不便宜，如果来路不明，车贩一般不敢收，肯定会通知警察。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">摩托车的去处无非几个，藏匿、销毁、出售、自留。如果后两种途径没有线索，这辆车就很难找到了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不过，凶手若是为车杀人，只藏或销毁就很奇怪。以车找凶手的线索走不通，郑舟在外的调查进展缓慢。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">放眼这片十多平方公里的老城区。在杀人分尸案发生的1998年，这里除了东边1公里外的煤矿，就是居住于案发棚户区的煤矿工人。煤矿东侧紧挨一条大河。上工向东，回家向西，人们每日往返在这条路上。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟走访时，街坊们没发现任何异常。就算有，连绵不绝的雨水也把痕迹洗刷干净了，“要不是清淤，尸体得烂成骨头渣子。”</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">查来查去，费劲不少，除了摸清几个去世尚未销户的人，再无异常。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">清查的阵势很大，就连我这个小孩子都能察觉到棚户区弥散着紧张的气氛。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" !important;\">这种时刻，人心不稳，郑舟甚至听说，有女人把案子往“男女关系”上猜，进而吓唬家里的男人：“下班赶紧回家，出去乱搞当心被人捅了丢沟里。”</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那时候查案的技术手段少，查案主要靠的还是警察自己的一双脚和遍布辖区的关系。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟手上的特情，多到需要用笔记本记。他早就想好了合适的人选——“老扁”。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这人贩过毒，火拼中被人抡起大铁锨拍了脑袋，以后从哪个角度观察，都能看出他的头异常扁平。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">虽然要调查“白面鬼”，郑舟并没有立刻行动。直到案发一个半月后，大沟分尸案逐渐淹没在街头巷尾的议论中。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">街坊们知道还没抓到凶手，但每天上矿回家的日子还得照常过。排污沟旁的大垃圾箱里，垃圾又多了起来。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟觉得火候到了。警方久久没有破案，凶手一定会放松警惕，该出击了。他托人给老扁带话儿。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当天下午，老扁慢腾腾地跟在郑舟身后，惴惴不安。郑舟的办公室离“小黑屋”不远——这是专给不听话的“顽固派”准备的，老扁在里面吃过亏。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟站在办公室门口，从裤兜摸出包“渡江”烟丢给老扁。老扁把烟揣到怀里，放心了大半，“大哥，啥事你就吱个声。”</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“谁最近手头宽绰？”郑舟把老扁请进办公室坐下，从抽屉里掏出半包“玉溪”，自己点燃一根，剩下的都丢给了老扁。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">90年代，吸毒者之间有股“义气劲”，总会相互匀几口毒品救急。共用注射器，也造成艾滋病、戊肝泛滥。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“这得给我两天时间查一查。只有实在没钱了，我们才找毒友匀一点。”老扁说得诚恳。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">过了三四天，老扁带来消息，毒鬼“马屎”最近好像特别阔。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟与马屎是老相识了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">马屎这老毒鬼，患有血液传染病，身上长满烂疮，整日讹人、偷盗。他总跑去亲戚家、邻居家借钱，不给就往屋里吐唾沫，或者掐把刀往手上划，故意让别人看见血。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">有一次，马屎朝抓捕他的警察吐唾沫。郑舟使出带风的大耳刮子，外加一顿踢打，灭了马屎的气焰。 </span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">军人出身的郑舟对待吸毒人员尤其粗暴。孙文泽曾担心这样打人迟早出事，劝过他，郑舟总是很气愤：“你知道什么！”</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这里的隐情孙文泽哪知道。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">80年代，郑舟参加对越“两山轮战”，排里有个小战士，二人感情深厚。小战士转业时放弃深造机会，回广西老家干边境缉毒警，被境外毒贩开枪击中腰部，再也离不开轮椅了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">从此郑舟对吸毒鬼子深恶痛绝。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">老扁说马屎不仅手里有很多货，还想搞一把火药枪。郑舟决定将马屎传唤到案。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那个晚上，马屎的邻居，刑警队联防队员传来消息，抓捕机会来了——马屎家灯亮了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">刑警队办公室里。抓捕组在研究行动方案，气氛异常紧张，特别是因为马屎手里可能有枪。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟沉默地坐在沙发上，认真地擦着枪——不是日常携带的五四式手枪，而是一把七九式轻型冲锋枪。郑舟找局长特批的。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这枪细长外形，折叠枪托，射速极快，单发准，全自动发射，20发弹匣眨眼就打完。这枪在从军多年的郑舟手里，基本上指哪打哪。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">夜深了。郑舟把冲锋枪背在身上，仿佛回到了前线。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">借着棚户房微弱的门头灯，郑舟带人深一脚浅一脚地走向马屎家的二层建筑。漆黑的巷子里，昏黄的灯光从没上锁的大红铁门透出。</span></section><section 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟一脚踢开大门，躺椅上的马屎吓了一大跳。他光着膀子，穿大裤头，正在柿子树下乘凉小酌。马屎一个激灵跃起，还带翻了躺椅、卤菜盘和酒瓶，一溜烟奔上楼。</span></section><section !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">郑舟持枪，率三人紧跟上楼。马屎跑进二楼屋里，传来一阵叮咣响。郑舟想到马屎可能搞到了火药枪，将冲锋枪顶上膛火，踹门进屋。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">屋里没开灯。月光下，马屎瘦弱的黑影站在窗边，他愣了几秒，从二楼一跃而下。他跳进齐腰的野草丛，用手拨拉着野草，一瘸一拐地往前奔跑。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: !important;\">胡小燕当场大哭，估计是担心自己吸毒的事情暴露，男友会和她分手。她看郑舟的眼神由害怕变成了恨，充满怒火，人在铁椅子上扭动，仿佛想和比她高半截的郑舟单挑。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, !important;\">胡小燕的伤口无比平整，一新一旧两道伤口横平竖直，连深浅都基本一致。这明显是拿刀比划半天，下决心呲溜一划形成的。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue !important;\">这道伤口无比刺眼，虽然血迹比对结果还没出来，但大家心里明白，胡小燕几乎没有作案的可能性。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb !important;\">郑舟很后悔没听孙文泽的劝，但他爱面子，又不好意思主动道歉。他连招呼都没打，就默默离开刑警队，去了三公里外的派出所工作。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">孙文泽一直看着赵庭，等他先开了口。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“你们老了，我也老了。这事该有结果了。”</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这些年，赵庭一直在学习法律，尤其进监狱之后，把阅览室里的刑法书翻遍了。他清楚，虽然没直接参与杀死吴军，但自己肯定犯了教唆杀人罪。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">赵庭毫不避讳地还原了排污沟分尸案的经过。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1988年，本地煤矿成为国家大型矿业单位，拥有将近三万职工，赵庭也是一名煤矿工人。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">他常光顾煤矿门口的小美容店。那时附近只有专门给男人修面、刮胡子、剪头的理发店。80年代末，自由恋爱很时髦，赵庭追求到年轻漂亮的女老板。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">赵庭爱赌钱，还喜欢在赌场“吸两口”。那年代人人谈毒色变，谁沾上这玩意，周围人厌弃，单位直接开除。 </span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1989年春天，清晨很冷。赵庭在麻将馆奋战一夜，顶着黑眼圈昏昏沉沉地走进矿场，躲进职工宿舍睡大觉。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">睡梦中，保卫科的人破门而入，赵庭被扭送派出所。因吸毒、赌博，他被劳教两年。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1991年，赵庭出狱。他失去工作，家人态度疏离。他还发现，自己好不容易追求到的女友，嫁给了同厂职工吴军。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">赵庭不在的两年，吴军马上填补了他的位置，对他的女友大献殷勤，成功挖了“墙角”。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">后来，当矿工的赌友告诉赵庭，他当年被抓，是因为被匿名电话举报，而举报人，就是吴军。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当年，吴军和赵庭在同一个厂里上班，但互相不熟悉。吴军看到赵庭的女朋友漂亮，开始留意赵庭的一举一动。他发现赵庭吸毒。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在80年代，吸毒、开除公职、戴绿帽子都是一等一的丢人事，而赵庭在同一时间都摊上了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">侦查员问赵庭，既然1991年就知道被吴军举报，还被抢了女朋友，为什么当时没实施杀人？</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, !important;\">赵庭被煤矿开除后，去过两广打工，后来回本市工地打小工，一直是孤家寡人。90年代，还在精神病院住过一阵，因为那里床位便宜。赵庭常年和满身泥灰的工友厮混，他因盗窃工地财物，进过两次看守所。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这些年，吴军却过得不错。赵庭每次和老朋友们喝酒，当年的三角关系总会被人拿出来调侃。赵庭不甘心，凭什么吴军的日子太平风光，自己却四处漂泊。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica !important;\">1998年夏天，赵庭在大坝上吹风醒酒，注意到一个在大坝上徘徊的瘦小男人。那人离自己不远不近。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans !important;\">正巧，吴军骑摩托车从坝上驶过，赵庭恨恨地看着吴军，等车灯变暗，吴军消失后，他收回目光，发现瘦小男人居然也那样望着吴军消失的方向。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" !important;\">赵庭走过去，递给瘦小男人一支烟，只试探了一句，就确定了他是陈学兵。赵庭把在脑中酝酿了无数遍的杀人抛尸计划，全教给了他。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica !important;\">他确定陈学兵不认识自己，只要判了陈学兵死罪，枪毙了他，自己就和排污沟分尸案彻底断绝了联系。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">听说陈学兵枪毙了，赵庭从广州回到老家，开始大大方方地在各个工地打工，过上他以为的安全生活。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“为什么两封匿名信之间隔了一个月？”当年那一个月可把刑警队折腾得不清。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui !important;\">“都一个月了，你们还没抓人，我等急了。”</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">孙文泽终于放下心来，警队里真的没有内鬼。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial !important;\">从1998到2014年，16年过去了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">他拨通了电话：“郑舟，案子破了，批刑拘吧。”</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">电话那头，郑舟“嗯”了一声。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"caret-color: rgb(136, 136, 136);color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif center rgb>▲</span></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"caret-color: rgb(136, 136, 136);color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif center rgb><br></span></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">看完这个故事，再跟大家介绍一下故事的发生地。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">那是一座位于江南丘陵的小城，由于煤炭储量特别丰富，还带着东北工业城市的厚重感。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"> </section><section style=\"white-space: normal;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">但煤矿是资源，也是原罪。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">村之间的械斗，黑社会的抢夺，本地人和外地移民的冲突，都和煤炭有脱不开的关系。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">煤矿工业给小城的变化就好像磁带的两面，A面是繁盛，B面则是血腥。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">作者蒋述在12岁之前，就住在煤矿工村附近，这里平房和棚户区交杂错落，治安乱的时候，一旦发生家族群架，几个出口都会被巨石沙包堵住，警车根本进不去。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">房前还发生了警匪枪战，79冲锋枪爆豆般的声音一夜没停；小学5年级的一个早晨，蒋述甚至见证了一场江湖仇杀的血腥现场。<br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"> </section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">但这座小城其实并不特殊，只是某个转型时期后，千万小城的缩影。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">这样故事在翻滚的时代浪潮中，发生在各地，故事里的人可以是任何人。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">也正因此，这座城市和城市里的人值得被记录。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"> </section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">蒋述说，他写下的故事里，有些人已经永远看不到这些文字了，而正是为了这些人在被遗忘之前，把这一切都记录下来。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\">如今这些故事，连同多年来对抗阴暗面的过程，也已经集结成书。</section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right:
